When you treat the disease of the mouse as we have said in the division of treatments, and it does not improve, then they resort to three methods of cauterization that are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant; et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos; et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule; et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	In this manner, there is a way to do three or four cauterizations, lining up according to the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the liver cauterization that we have mentioned before; and do not press your hand on the whole cauterization, and let the hairs be on its back; and another way of cauterization is to heat the cauterization that has two needles, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder; and lift the curtain that is near the mouse, or where the pain of the ear comes from the right side, and let the elevations that you lift the curtain according to the curve, according to the length of the body, and the cauterization should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After you have boiled the two needles until the one that is held in the other part is perceived to be hot, then remove the cautery, and thus you will have four. And if you see, then cauterize the entire cautery with three needles.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has been broken by long tension, and this is also useful for the other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	of hydropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterizing does not work for hydropsy, except in the manner that is called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat it according to the methods that we have mentioned in divisions, and your treatment does not work, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries around the belly, and one above the stomach, and one above the liver, and one above the spleen, and two behind the back on the spine, and one at the worst place; and let the cauteries be close to the skin where the patient is most affected.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After leaving the fire cautery for a short time to cool, and not neglecting the care of the wound after the cauterization; and healing will be hastened, and together with God's help, both intentions will be achieved.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the fire cautery for the abdomen is like the one we have shown before; and for the back, it is an olive branch, as it was mentioned before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the feet are swollen and have a yellowish discharge, it is necessary to cauterize above the back of the foot between the auricular and annular; and release your hand with the cauterization to return.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, thus avoiding the yellowish parts, and let the cauteries be done according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After making two incisions on each leg at the tip of a sharp knife; and let the cauteries be long, one behind the knee in front and the other in front of the knee on the leg; and leave the cauteries hanging longer than to cure, so that the wound may heal from the inside; after curing the other treatments that we have said.
de la menoison	of the calf
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the belly solution comes from cold and moisture, as long as the retentive and digestive virtues that are in the stomach and in the intestines are blocked, and cannot be cured by other methods of treatment; and you see the patient suffering greatly and with great pain, then make a large cauterization above the stomach according to what he has spoken of before or the stomach cauterization, and circulate the cauterization around it; and four cauterizations around the belly subtly to all the subtle clavile cauterizations, and two cauterizations above the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient is suffering from pain, then perform fire cauterization on the knuckle, and one cauterization on each joint, and two small cauterizations on the stomach below the large one, for the cure is beneficial when it has good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of worms
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the worms are deeply rooted, or one or more, and are ancient and are large humors that are cold and moist and corrupted, and are treated as we have said in divisions, and it does not improve, then perform cauterizations: three on the spine of the back, which is placed gradually and gradually in triangular, and one cauterization outside the abdomen two doses; and if you think that the stomach is cooled, and the food does not cook, and one sees the face swells, then apply a large cauterization on the stomach, as it has been said before, and one on the liver, and one on the mouse all over the cauterization clavile; and leave the cauterization open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, the limb when it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the cartilage which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you cut the cartilage, if the cauterizing iron seems like a razor, and then put it all burned on top of the cartilage cut; and let your hand be so that the cauterizer comes to the base of the wound, from which the blood flows; do this once or twice, and if there is much cartilage, cauterize each part as we have said; after the treatment of painful swelling until it is healed; and if you cauterize with a large cauterizing iron on top of the cartilage, it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	of a badly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the pain cannot be relieved by a surgeon or incision, as we will explain in its place, then illness comes that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When any fistula comes, and it is inflamed and discharged putrid and corrupted moisture, then you must apply a fine tent to the whole of it, and guard that you wash away the entire tent as much as it has.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After heating the cauterizer as if it were a razor, and pushing it into the fistula according to the amount that the tent has entered, and then start the cauterization again until those parts are burned and corrupted, once or twice, or three times, depending on the amount of pain; and guard against burning the nerves that are nearby, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes to the center of the bladder and the intestine, then guard against these areas, and only perform surgery where there is nourishment, and think that it is not healed; after curing the area for as long as it is healthy, and if the areas are still sore, and the matter is removed along with the tension, then wash that area completely clean; and if the matter is not removed, then wash that area thoroughly, and corrupt the bone at the source; and thus like one of those that we will say in its area.
de la maladie des reins	of the kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain from the kidneys comes, and with great swelling, and does not take medicine, then it is necessary that you burn them on both sides of the kidneys with the clavile cautery that we have already mentioned; and if we cauterize in the middle, then there will be three cauterizations in a line, and they will be greater.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is small and weak from dryness and moisture, and the pain retains urine, then perform cauterization in the part before the bladder, where the hair begins to grow on either side, and each cautery should be as long as a pin; and also perform cauterization before the back, or twice if you have need; and let the cauteries be in the form of a cross as previously mentioned.
de la marris	of the marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the marsh is cold and wet, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are corrupted and late in blooming; and when they come, they cause great pain: then it is necessary to perform three cauterizations around the womb, as we have mentioned with the cautery of the bladder, and two cauterizations before the back; and let the cauteries be in the form of a cross, as we have mentioned.
de la hainche	of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends to the hip bone, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and it is found that the lower parts of the thighs are twisted, then you must cauterize the misalignment above the hip bone with a cautery like a circle, and sign before the joint around the hip bone as it turns, so that the hip bone is inside the circle; and if it is such a cauterization as that which has been cauterized in the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this cauterization is not present, then make three cauterizations of the large olive grove, and let the cauterizations be done as all the others; and the care until they are healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the groin of the hip, and it is from cold and moisture, and the pain is relieved by what we have said in the division and the cure does not help, and the disease is ancient: therefore it is necessary that you purge the pain of heavy humors with fetid pills, or other good-smelling pills similar.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the cauterization; and the manner of the cauterization is thus: it is to say together with medicines burning, and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire cauterization is thus in many ways, some of which are: that you cauterize above the groin of the hip three triangular cauterizations in this form, and do good depth and great, and have between each cauterization a space of the size of a finger, and let the cauterizations olive-oil; never made on one cautery in the middle of the hip, because it is there four in this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see, the cauterize with the cautery in a circle as we have previously mentioned in the dislocation of the shoulder; but do it in a different manner so that the circle contains the entire shoulder, and all the tendons are burned away.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way to do it in surgery, when the pain remains in the shoulder and does not reach the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if it comes to the thigh and the leg, then make two cautery marks where the pain is located, and one cautery mark above the ankle four fingers wide, on the right side; and let the cautery be sharp, and burn away the tendons; and if the patient feels that the pain extends to the foot or near the knee, then cauterize where he feels the pain three fingers or four at the cautery called "finger".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the craft is to do more; and if the pain is from the groin to the thigh, then cauterize with a surgical or circular cautery, and be very careful in all your cauterizations that you do not leave the cautery for too long, burning the nerves and large arteries, and causing greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	I myself have seen many who have cauterized above the ankle bone, and left it for so long that the leg was completely paralyzed, and the foot as well, and all the bones were perforated and rotten.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a bout of vomiting where they lost their life.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in both parts together, use cauterization on one and the other, as follows.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the wise say in the cauterization of the loins, regarding this matter, use a needle as thick as a navillon of a finger, or slightly less, and pierce through and from one to the other at a distance equal to the quantity of a thumb; and the piercings should be over two parts, and also like a comb, and there should be a good needle. And this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it be cauterized until it is completely red and has a sense of heat, then place it on the board of the back misaligned, and turn it over to the healthy side; and cauterize once with the cautery and leave it for three days; and then apply a plaster of butter, and leave the wound open long; after the care of ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasis says that we use this cautery little because of its fearful appearance, and few see those who use it; however, this is a good cautery, which can bear the pain, and where it takes effect.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The cauteries of burning medicine are such that you make an instrument with interstices on the edge of the door, and it is either of iron or of tin at a length, and in the top has II us, and each amount of the groats of a dozen; and they are open below and above, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After putting the bandage of the back to the misaligned part lying on its side, and quickly place your hand over the bandage of the back; then pour between the two circles of hot water that is heated at the fire I poc, and let it stand for an hour, and suffer the misaligned parts the heat and the burning of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is true that there is also cauterization with fire; and when the cauterizations have passed, lift your hand with the instrument and gently raise the waist from the wound, and leave it for three days, and put butter on it until the black scab from the burn is removed; and let it rest for three days until the inflammation has subsided; and this would be the last aid after the cure of boils as long as they are healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, make the instrument that you have made for the waist again; and this is the way of the hot wound, and I have written it in the treatment of the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take equal parts of quicklime and fresh chalk, and grind them together, and put them in a new earthenware pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Then, if there is a small hole left, unless the point of a razor can fill it; and put that pot in another well-ploughed pot, and put on top of the lime and chalk and add boiling water until you have the second layer of powder as you have before; and let it stand until all the water drips out and the pot is ploughed, then take all the water and pour it over the lime and chalk as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And if it is very painful and administered in the form of medical works and cauteries of other members, for it does great harm like fire, and if it is with other medicines that are well cauterized on the back, such as mustard plasters and chalk mixed with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	Galen tells us of a cure where some were cured of the pain in the back and sciatica, and they were much healed, and said that no other cure was done, and that they were well after once this cure was made, and he was bathed as he teaches thereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And in a similar manner, you should apply a fresh, green willow leaf, and grind it thoroughly with a little grease, and place it on the back, on the thigh, and on the leg where the pain is located, and tie it; and let him leave it for three hours and by the quantity that the pains no longer feel the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him enter a warm bath until the heart is slightly warmed, and make him lie down, and the pain will go away completely and will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And warn that no one should use such remedies with cauterization unless it is after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dioscorides says that when the vein of the sciatic nerve is cauterized with burning goat's fat, it helps a lot; and the cautery should be made in this way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take another and beat it with old oil, and place it on the sinus that is between the thumb and the other one which is called the forefinger.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	Then take some dry goat's fat and put it in the fire until it becomes charcoal, and place it on the linen, and leave it until it is soaked; and do this again and again, and do not stop doing this until you think that it has reached the back, and that the pain has ceased; and this way of cauterizing is called "goat's fat cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain of two days
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or from impact or from too great evacuation, or from similar matters that are expanded and cold, none of these remedies is worth cauterization, because it is better to wait for the one who has just been infused with cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary to apply foul-smelling pills or similar matters on top of the back, where the pain is located, three lines wide, and in each line V cauteries or more according to the potency and quantity that the pain can bear; and let the cauteries be made with the cauterizer called "pointed"; and if you see, make III cauteries or IV at the middle cauterizer according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	Many times this disease comes to small children, and the signs of onset are that they have a stiff neck when moving, and fear; and you feel in the last spinous process of the back and in us the appearance that comes above the other spinous processes.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you want to cure it, if you cauterize with the fire cautery in this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the fire cautery grips each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, then cauterize around the spine with the fire cautery holding two or three lines apart, and they are the points close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the patient has been treated according to what we have said, and you should not administer cauterization in a place that is swollen with a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the pain of the joints is from moisture that is spread to each limb of the body, and when the pain comes in a sudden way, which is called "gout" properly, and when it is caused by cold and medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauterization in this manner: apply the most cauterization around the joint, and let the cauterizing oil be applied according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	If there is doubt that you can hold the face of the patient during the cauterization, then perform the entire cauterization with the claim "not to touch".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pain comes from the jaw and other joints, and this happens often, then perform cauterization on each jaw with three or four cauteries of each part, during the entire olive oil cauterization; and if you have more skill, do more, but do not hold your hand further than the span of the healer's arm.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pain descends to the jaw and back, then administer the cauterization that we have mentioned in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, make points around the fingernails; and if they remain not in the hands, make points over each joint and over the hair of the hand; and if the pains come just above the elbow or just above the shoulder, cauterize each part, and give good management to the patient and proper medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give good management and purge the humor, it will be healed with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the breaking of the tooth
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the breaking of the tooth occurs in anger, and the bile descends to the intestines and this is new, then it is necessary that when you see it to be healed, that it not move much that day; and that it use things that relieve the stomach, so that the pain does not come from its belly; afterwards make it sit on its back between your hands, and command it to tuck its tail as long as the bile is restored, and rub it against your fingers, and sign over the breaking of the tooth above the bone of the thumb, and a sign that is similar to half a circle above the body; then heat the cautery with this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until it is white and sweats senselessly.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then remove the mud from the joint; and the ministrant stains his hand above that they do not return backward; and work well the thighs at the shoulder, and put disinfectant on him some cussin and some serum above the thighs, and the other above the lowest which stains his hands; then put the cauterizer above the sign all over your hand, and the one that is right and the one that is long as you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, start again another until you come close to the bone; and be careful that the mud does not come out when you do the cauterizer; that you do not burn it; and that by this the pain does not kill him, or any other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And when you do not reach the bone with the fire cautery, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And the cauterizer for children should be thin according to their size, and for large people, also large according to their size; after three days, care for the leg of the fire cautery until the burn is healed; then care for other wounds as long as they are healthy, and let the hairs lie flat on their back for forty days so that the wound is well healed; and it is important that their movements be restricted for a long time, so that the blisters do not form when they move around.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After forty days, when he wishes to rise, he should be given a well-made bandage for forty more days; and he should have good rest, working little and avoiding too much drinking and eating, and too much heat; and if he follows this advice, he will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will tell you about the cure after cutting into his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the tearing of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When tears come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow any more, then apply the fire cautery according to its quantity, and let it be the third part of the cure; after the cure, according to what we have said; and none of the ancients have said that one should cauterize at the cautery at three angles in this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but the first sign is the shoulder blade sticking out and make a line along the width of the tear, and another behind, and with your hand hold the entire cauterizing iron.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and more gentle.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, whether it falls or pierces, and this pain lasts long, and the medicine of healing does not help, then it is necessary to cauterize with the cautery called «pons», and the cauteries according to the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and its strength and its position of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first cauterization is healthy, it's good; if not, start another cauterization above the first one, as it is customary that the patient should die at the member that is nearest, for which you must perform the cauterizations until the hairs are healed.
de meselerie	of mesmerism
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The mesenteries are often helped by cauterization with great help, and immediately the disease that comes from the putrefaction of fluids and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	If you see the cauterization, take care if the disease is at the beginning, and if it has been cured according to what we have said in the previous division, and does not remain or settle, and you doubt that the corruption will not spread throughout the whole body, then perform two cauterizations: I on the forehead, and the other towards the front at the end of the eyebrows; and II above the two horns, and I behind the tail; and let your hand be as close to the bone as possible, and as long as the scabs come out so that the vapors of the large humors can escape; and cauterize again on the mouse according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And if the injury is widely spread; and it is clearly manifest, so you should cauterize with these cautery methods that we have said or chief, and the cauterizing in the middle of the nose, and two above the spine of the neck, and six above the spine of the back, and one large on the buttocks and one other below, and two on the shoulders, and two on the elbows, and two on the knees, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the fissures of the hands; and beware of the nerves that are above the bones, that you do not burn them; and never make a cauterization on the bone of the wrist, and one on the bone of the stomach, and one on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And the more you do cauterization, the less you should do assistance, and move it; and know that the pains are not felt at cauterization as they are felt by the healthy one, because the body is already corrupt.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It should be that the cauterization is large and small according to the members and the joints, according to what you will find in the manner of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the wound with flour and honey and other cures until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When inflammation comes to any member and is cured with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healed, then do cauterization on the member according to its size and smallness; and let the cauterization be a little inside the surface of the cure; then the cure of inflammation until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And never cauterize with the hand and the foot and the back, at the end of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus it is stopped by the inflammation; and in any case do not interfere unless one knows the members and the outlets of the moving nerves of the body.
de albaras	et de l’albaras
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "albaras" is awakened, and medical treatment does not help, then cauterize with a cautery a little in advance, according to the quantity of the spice that cures, until the swelling is stopped, and its color is restored; then treat with flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and honey from colonies and honey from bees, each in equal parts; and mix all together, and apply to the wound, and bind it to the body until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of chancre by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a chancre first appears, and it is seen to stop spreading, then cauterize it with the cauterizing iron that seems like a circle, all around the edge of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And it is said by many wise people that one should also make the cauterizing iron in the middle of the chancre; and I do not think this is good, because I believe it should not be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have never seen it happen; and a better thing is that it be cauterized all around, with the cauterizing iron that is called «circle», as we have said in many places.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When anyone has a disease called "adubelati", and it lingers or dies slowly due to the excess it causes or because of its age when they are very old and have little blood, or due to tension; then you see it hastening to die: therefore cauterize around much with small cauteries pricking; afterwards leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing with the whole cautery, then warm the cautery from where this is its form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" until the cauteries have pierced the skin, and let the cauteries be such that the hairs feel afterwards in a similar manner as the course of the porridge is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure until they are perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The cure of fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing other than a certain amount of member, for it twists the members as if the dry reeds were twisted.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the leg that can suffer cauterization along with fire, then heat the cauteries a little and greatly, according to what is necessary for the leg or the disease; afterwards cauterize all parts until you have reached all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that everything that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then leave it three days, and place the wounds with oil, suffering from burns until the scabs of fire are removed, and all corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of burns, it generates fever.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that healthy fever does not arise, it is good; and if not, then restart the cauterization on the part that remains corrupted.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this method has never been treated with medicine in place of fire cauterization; but all the same, fire cauterization is of greater help, and I have already given the cure for medicine fever in the division: take it when you have need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the pearls that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often times, when the feet are not washed properly, a disease arises which is called "clos" according to our understanding, and it is a great harm that blackens the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauteries for this disease are in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cauterization, and water cauterization with hot iron.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is that you heat the cautery as if it were a pen of feather, and it should be made of good iron at the measure that it can penetrate the nail from all parts, and that it has thin edges; afterwards, put it all hot on top of the nail, and turn your hand around the nail until it reaches the bottom of the nail; and leave it thus for three days until it begins to rot; then make an ointment of wild herbs ground with oil, and leave the ointment all night, and the nail will fall off and be extracted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the limb with oil, using a warm poultice until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are converted by the previous corpse, and often in hands and feet, it is necessary that you use cauterization with hot iron; and it is in this way: take a needle of iron or steel, or a quill pen, and place it on top of the nail and the skin, that is to say, pricking the warts; then place the needle on top so that it penetrates all around, then put a little hot water in a pot, and hold your hand tightly, and press your hand back and forth so that the edge of the needle reaches the root of the nail, and find the hot water way deep to the root; and let the pain of the hot water for one hour; then leave it like this, and it will all fall off at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Next, do another one until you have treated all those that are in the body, then cure the wounds caused by a chariot.
li cure dou trembler	the cure of the trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When anyone trembles from cold or from a quarter fever or other, it is necessary that you make four cautery or four above the spine of the back, one cautery between each spine; and one cautery on the chest, and one over the stomach with the cauterizing oil; if this allows them to tremble, and hurries the health from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pus-filled boils
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No times appear by previous wounds, or pustules that come from large corrupted matters.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary to the first when they appear that one make a cauterization above each head of the pustule: a subtle cautery of mullein, of which the point is grasped in the fire, or of the root of aristolochia long, or at the lenticular cauterization.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And no times cauterize at the beginning when they appear, in this manner, and it cannot grow new ones, but is broken down the excess from which they come, and are healed; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Often there is great bleeding from the cut artery at the wound that comes from the surroundings, or at the incision of the abscess, or in the fire cauterization of the limb, and similar things; and it is a very painful thing to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And in any case, when this happens, you must quickly place your finger on the wound of the vein, and hold it tightly until the bleeding is stopped, and no more blood comes out; then put the cauterizing irons of olive oil several times, both small and large, until they are all red; then insert I, or a great or small one according to the wound and the limb in which the artery is located, and place the cauterizing iron on that vein where you hold your finger, and hold it until the bleeding is stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if the first one fails and you lift your second hand over the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, then quickly take another from the ones that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not cease to do this one after the other until the wound is cauterized; and be careful not to burn the nerve that is next to it, and that no other harm comes over the injury; and make sure that when the artery is not cut, that you cannot extinguish it immediately when the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods that we have mentioned: or by cauterization, or by extraction when it is not yet treated, or by a very thin thread, or by medicines placed on top that have power to stop bleeding.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever manages the tightening of knots closely with cloth or metal things over, or other similar things, does not benefit if not properly.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and they do not have any medicine present, they should place their index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and tightly bind it as much as possible above the wound and above the vein; and they should not move it, but keep it moist with cold water often until it is congealed and swollen and bound; and make inquiries about what they need for cauterization and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book of remedies for tails
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have told you in the first chapter all diseases for which it is necessary to use fire cauterization, or burning medicine, and the symptoms and causes and instruments and forms of cauteries; and I will put this chapter about the lower jaw from the feet, and I will go to this chapter by the same way because one finds more easily what one wants.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And therefore when I begin this chapter, it is necessary, dear son, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and for this reason it requires greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many ways of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	If they come from such people who are so with their illness that they die immediately because of the danger they find in their disease, and the greatness of its wickedness; and of these one must have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And of these, there are those who give you their sense, and say: "Wait, I am hurt"; and the illness is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	It does not matter whether you grant your consent to those who come to you with this manner, but place greater trust in your honor than in your desires, and do not open rashly but wisely of that of which you are certain, and which you have taken and lost; and use prediction and indication in the treatment of your illnesses for salvation to be converted; and this will help you to acquire good reputation, glory, and memory for a long time.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lords grant you good understanding and uprightness, and if you wish to breathe from the Holy Spirit's breath, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered you this chapter by examining other chapters, according to what is before the chapter on cautery, which I have advised from the beginning to the end, because you will find it more easily what you will have to do.
dou chief plein d’aigue	The main full of sharp
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	That this disease often comes to children at birth, and when the child's head is held too tightly; and sometimes it comes because of a recurring cause that one is not aware of.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this disease elsewhere than in children, and all those that I have seen were quickly killed by it; and because it seems to me that it is better to prevent the work in such cases.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw a child who was suffering from a sharp pain, and the head was growing bigger each day until it could no longer bear it; and because of the moisture, it died, and this moisture is gathered outside the bone above the sinus, between the skin and the bone; and the treatments are such that if the moisture is between the skin and the bone, and the abscesses are small, you should make a large incision in the head; and it should be as long as half of our nose, so that the moisture can flow out; and take out the form of the spatula.
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more severe, and the abscess is larger, then make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is outside the bone, and the signs that you see the commissures of the joint are open on each side, and the sharp pain persists as you press it with your hand inside, and it does not respond: then it is necessary to make three incisions in the following manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After the incisions are dressed with bandages and powders, and you put wine and oil, and leave it to dry for five days; then remove it, and treat the wound with compresses and counterirritants, and keep the joint immobile, and gradually introduce dry moisture as much as the limb is comfortable and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way of incision is that you look at the size of the abscess and the assembly of the needle; for it is never in front, never behind, never to the right, and never to the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Therefore, cut the size of the abscess and fill the needle, and make the incision according to what you have the ability to do; and be careful not to cover the artery; and if there is blood flow, it may cause the wounds to die from the flow of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of return
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When it has any disease called "cataract" in the eyes or the pupil, and the disease is ancient, and the medical treatment does not help much, then the cure is to cauterize with what is covered over the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Therefore, when you see the hairs, it is necessary that the hairs make their way back to their head; after that, rub the skin with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then hold the hairs against the cloth in all directions; then look where the wound bleeds, and the ears on both sides are not far away, and they are quickly replaced; then sign the ears with a sharp instrument, then cover both with a piece of linen cloth, as wide as two parts of the head, until the wound comes out to the bone, and it should be through the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, push the sharp instrument away from the artery and cover it above, cutting in the same way as it should be across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, if blood spurts out continuously from above.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And if the artery does not open when felt, it is necessary to measure the quantity of space for three fingers, then bend and cut to the bone; and what amount of sane to put out depends on six centimeters, and perhaps a little more or less, according to what the wounds can suffer, and the replenishment of the artery; then look at the wound: if it remains above the bone point, if the cope that we have sewn does not come out, then strain the wound and bind, and the treatment of ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of a migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an ancient migraine comes, and the cautery is not effective, due to the moisture of tears and the heat in the temples and the old pain and similar things, and it is treated with methods of medical treatment and nothing seems to help, then we should cauterize the arteries of the temples, as we have mentioned.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of their extraction is that the hairs of his temples are pulled back, and one should listen to the artery that opens in the temple, because it opens well by its pulsation, and it is only slightly replaced in some people who are too cold; and if it is replaced, then one should strain the skin with some cloths, then rub the skin with some rough cloth, and heat the skin with hot water until the artery clearly opens; then take the sponge of which this form is made:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	Then slightly scrape the skin until you reach the artery, then cut it upwards with pincers, and remove all the threads that are attached to each part; if the artery is thin, turn it to the point of the needle, then cover that part according to the amount of the two chapters.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not covered, it will not heal at all.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And draw out six drops of blood from the vein, just to the third; and if the artery is large, it is necessary to tie it in two places with a strong silk thread, which does not allow any blood to come before the scab of the wound, and prevents the bleeding; then cover the excess that is between the two threads in the same hour, and then, if you see, if you cauterize the wound with the cautery knife just up to the bone until the chapters are covered; and this is the best work, if the hairs do not have fever and he is of hot constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For the fire cautery is to finish the moistures: because it is the greatest help for moistures.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	For the extraction of arteries, it is necessary to fill the wound with old cotton and place dry bandages on top; and when they are removed, apply dry medicines that create heat and bandages until they are healed; and if there is no bleeding from the artery, as much as you work, you must quickly cover it with a cautery, or you fill the wound with vinegar and hold it in your hand that the bleeding does not stop, and freeze the wound with cold water until it stops, and hold it tightly; and what is slower and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein of this cautery cutting from II parts, but the cutting should be well done to last longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	When the instruments are too tight, it holds less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus; et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it should have between the two knives a space of large diameter, and then when you have signified to fill the two grooves, and you melt the hot iron above so that it reaches the bone, and cope the vein in two grooves; and they should be separated between the two wounds because there is no surety of this cautery at all; and this is the form of the cauterization:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears of the eyes are flowing down the veins that are above the testicle of the chief of the phallus, and it does not profit much from medical care, and you see the face of the pain twisted, and feels like a throbbing; and it is often held and moist so that the hair of the papers is soaked, and the papers are discolored, and burned by the heat of the tears, if there is need for this cure.
